itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🌍 Streamlit-ladybug-Tools-V3.0 🐞</h1><a id="user-content--streamlit-ladybug-tools-v30-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🌍 Streamlit-ladybug-Tools-V3.0 🐞" href="#-streamlit-ladybug-tools-v30-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">项目简介 📖</h2><a id="user-content-项目简介-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 项目简介 📖" href="#项目简介-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">作为西建大建筑学专业的毕业生，我在学习建筑物理和建筑与城市气候课程时，逐渐接触到了一些能够有效服务于绿色建筑设计的软件和工具。然而，许多设计师和建筑学生在面对形式设计和建筑性能策略时，常常遇到零散且难以解析的问题。这些问题虽然关系到项目的长效节能和环境融合度，却往往被忽视。</p>
<p dir="auto">为了解决这些痛点，我意识到需要一个既专业又便捷的工具，能够将气候数据和绿色建筑技术结合起来。经过对现有绿色建筑设计软件和工具的研究，我决定开发一个全新的工具。这个工具应当具备以下特点：</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>🌏 <strong>全球化</strong>：用户可以随时获取全球任何地区的气候数据。</li>
<li>📊 <strong>直观性</strong>：以图表形式生动展现专业数据。</li>
<li>🤖 <strong>智能化</strong>：自动生成被动式设计策略和气候指标评价。</li>
<li>🌐 <strong>开放性</strong>：接受用户建议，持续改进。</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">主要功能 ✨</h2><a id="user-content-主要功能-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 主要功能 ✨" href="#主要功能-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>🌐 <strong>全球气象数据查询与分析</strong>：涵盖被动式策略、气温、风速风向、湿度、天空覆盖率、照度和辐射等多项数据。</li>
<li>🤖 <strong>人工智能总结与建议</strong>：基于分析结果提供绿建建议。</li>
<li>📊 <strong>灵活的图表调整</strong>：用户可自由选择月份和图表样式。</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">主要特色 💡</h2><a id="user-content-主要特色-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 主要特色 💡" href="#主要特色-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>🌏 <strong>全球数据在线调用</strong>：随时获取任何地区的气候数据。</li>
<li>🧠 <strong>智能分析与建议</strong>：基于绿建知识库提供合理建议。</li>
<li>🖼️ <strong>用户友好界面</strong>：直观的图表展示，易于操作。</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">版本更新 🔄</h2><a id="user-content-版本更新-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 版本更新 🔄" href="#版本更新-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">与2.0版本相比，3.0版本进行了全面的重构和优化：</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>🔧 <strong>代码重构</strong>：删除冗余代码，提升代码可读性。</li>
<li>🚀 <strong>性能提升</strong>：迁移至高性能服务器。</li>
<li>🎨 <strong>自定义色卡</strong>：新增自定义色卡功能。</li>
<li>🧩 <strong>人工智能模型优化</strong>：结合实际地理信息进行更合理的分析。</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">安装步骤 🛠️</h2><a id="user-content-安装步骤-️" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 安装步骤 🛠️" href="#安装步骤-️"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">直接使用🌐</h3><a id="user-content-直接使用" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 直接使用🌐" href="#直接使用"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">本地部署🗃️</h3><a id="user-content-本地部署️" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 本地部署🗃️" href="#本地部署️"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>克隆仓库：
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="git clone https://github.com/Zoumachuan/Streamlit-ladybug-Tools-V3.0"><pre>git clone https://github.com/Zoumachuan/Streamlit-ladybug-Tools-V3.0</pre></div>
</li>
<li>修改配置：
修改 <code>config.py</code> 中的 <code>OPENAI_API_HOST</code> 和 <code>OPENAI_API_KEY</code>。</li>
<li>创建虚拟环境并安装依赖：
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
pip install -r requirements.txt"><pre>python3 -m venv venv
<span class="pl-c1">source</span> venv/bin/activate
pip install -r requirements.txt</pre></div>
</li>
<li>运行项目：
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="streamlit run main.py"><pre>streamlit run main.py</pre></div>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">使用 Docker 🐳</h3><a id="user-content-使用-docker-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 使用 Docker 🐳" href="#使用-docker-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>克隆仓库：
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="git clone https://github.com/Zoumachuan/Streamlit-ladybug-Tools-V3.0"><pre>git clone https://github.com/Zoumachuan/Streamlit-ladybug-Tools-V3.0</pre></div>
</li>
<li>修改配置：
修改 <code>docker-compose.yaml</code> 中的 <code>OPENAI_API_HOST</code> 和 <code>OPENAI_API_KEY</code>。</li>
<li>启动 Docker 容器：
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="docker-compose up -d"><pre>docker-compose up -d</pre></div>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">贡献指南 🤝</h2><a id="user-content-贡献指南-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 贡献指南 🤝" href="#贡献指南-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">欢迎各位开发者提交PR！我对Python的使用尚不熟练，期待与绿建行业的同仁和爱好者们共同完善并扩展这个项目。</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">项目结构 🗂️</h2><a id="user-content-项目结构-️" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 项目结构 🗂️" href="#项目结构-️"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>charts/</code> 存放各种图表生成函数
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>humidity_chart.py</code> 用于生成湿度图 💧</li>
<li><code>illuminance_chart.py</code> 用于生成照度图 💡</li>
<li><code>passive_strategies_chart.py</code> 用于生成被动式策略图 🌱</li>
<li><code>radiation_chart.py</code> 用于生成辐射图 ☀️</li>
<li><code>sky_cover_chart.py</code> 用于生成天空覆盖率图 ☁️</li>
<li><code>temperature_chart.py</code> 用于生成温度图 🌡️</li>
<li><code>wind_chart.py</code> 用于生成风玫瑰图 🌬️</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>utils/</code> 存放各种数据处理函数
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>chart_generator.py</code> 用于图表生成 📈</li>
<li><code>data_loader.py</code> 用于读取EPW文件 📂</li>
<li><code>data_processor.py</code> 用于数据处理 🔄</li>
<li><code>file_manager.py</code> 用于文件管理 🗃️</li>
<li><code>openai_integration.py</code> 用于人工智能分析 🤖</li>
<li><code>template_base.py</code> 用于色卡管理 🎨</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>config.py</code> 配置文件 ⚙️</li>
<li><code>dockerfile</code> Docker 配置文件 🐋</li>
<li><code>main.py</code> 主程序入口 🚪</li>
<li><code>requirements.txt</code> 依赖库列表 📜</li>
</ul>
